Inspecting Yangtze River Pilot Licenses 145

There has been no regulation of Yangtze River pilots, which has left the gateways to key inland fortresses wide open. At this time of serious foreign aggression, the government, recognizing the deep and significant connection between this and wartime operations and national defense, has ordered that all practicing pilots must obtain a practicing certificate, and has ordered the Jianghai and Jianghan Customs, as well as the customs along the Yangtze River, to strictly inspect the pilot's licenses when ships arrive at their respective ports.

Northern Region

Overview of Relief Work for Women and Children 146

The Shanghai Chinese Child Welfare Association previously dispatched Deputy Director-General Chen Tiesheng to the northern war zone to work with all sectors to carry out relief work for women and children, as reported previously. It is now learned that Mr. Chen has safely arrived in the north and is working hard on the project. There are now more than 50,000 refugees in Beiping, with women and children accounting for 80 to 90 percent of them. Apart from a small number of middle-class families who are staying in hotels (some are staying with relatives), the majority are living in the open air, exposed to the wind and rain, in a very pitiful situation. Through the efforts of Mr. Wang Xizhi, director of the Child Welfare Group of the Beiping Church Federation, eight shelters have been established one after another. The funds are mostly provided by Mr. Qu Wenliu and Mr. Feng Yangshan, representatives of the Northeast Refugee Relief Association. Mr. Zhang Yuanshan has also opened two shelters, which can accommodate thousands of people. In Tianjin, the Christian Relief Association has been organized and has sheltered more than 36,000 refugees, including more than 10,000 children. In Tongzhou, there are more than 20,000 women and children seeking refuge, with more than 12,000 being sheltered in the Luhe Middle School and more than 6,000 being sheltered in Catholic churches, Red Swastika Society shelters, mosques, etc. In addition, the Christian Girls' School and the Xuedaoyuan Church are also sheltering more than 1,700 people. Mr. Feng Yangshan has allocated 32,000 jin of rice to be transported to Tongzhou to provide relief to the refugees. Mr. Chen Tiesheng, on behalf of the Child Welfare Association, has also donated 500 yuan to purchase various types of infant food for approximately 3,600 boys and girls aged one to five, which is being distributed in various shelters.

The City Chamber of Commerce Petitions for Interpretation

Doubts About the Statute of Limitations for Accounts 147

The City Chamber of Commerce sent a petition to the Judicial Yuan yesterday, stating that it was a petition for an issue. According to a letter from the Silk and Satin Trade Association, and in turn, a letter from the Xulun Store Group, the letter states that the amount of credit accounts issued by the group's members has been very large over the years. Traditionally, accounts have been settled three times a year. However, some customers may be staying in other cities or have gone overseas, and due to various special circumstances, they may only settle their accounts after three or five years. According to commercial practice, customer credit, and mutual understanding, this has been the case for a long time. Recently, however, a few customers who owe debts cite the

Two-Year Statute of Limitations to Resist Merchants' Claims for Payment. Such fraud and breach of faith, if this precedent is set, it is feared that the victims in the business world will be countless. Therefore, we earnestly request your association to quickly forward a letter to the City Chamber of Commerce, requesting the Judicial Yuan to interpret Article 127, Item 8 of the Civil Code, as to whether the two-year statute of limitations applies to the loans taken by customers from merchants in the silk and satin industry, and whether there are other remedies available to protect the legal interests of merchants, in case debtors insist on relying on this provision to avoid payment, and set a precedent that would not only cause great harm to the silk and satin industry, but would also affect the entire national economy. We earnestly beseech your assistance in forwarding this request for interpretation, and we will be deeply grateful. In view of this, the Chamber of Commerce believes that merchants rely entirely on credit when extending credit, and that if this precedent is set, creditors will lose their protection, while debtors will have a basis for evasion. If this continues, what business can be done? According to the circumstances described in the letter, we must urgently send a letter to your esteemed association, requesting you to quickly forward it to the Judicial Yuan to request an interpretation of the meaning and scope of Article 127, Item 8 of the General Principles of the Civil Code, so that there will be something to follow and to protect the legal interests of merchants. We will be publicly grateful. When the association was instructed to supplement the situation of whether a notice of account has been sent, regarding the so-called "excuse", whether it means that they are unable to repay and are requesting an extension to the next installment, if that is the case, it is considered an admission under Article 129, Item 2 of the same law, the statute of limitations is of course interrupted, and they should supplement their statements layer by layer, so as to forward the request for interpretation. Now, the trade association has replied, stating that member stores invariably sent billing notices to their credit customers at set intervals, without interruption. However, sending billing notices at these intervals is customary for all stores in the country, and there is no receipt or evidence of this. As for customers who have not settled their accounts, they not only send billing notices at set intervals, but also send personnel to collect the debts on a monthly basis. That is, they have never given up on exercising their right to claim. However, debtors often delay and postpone payment arbitrarily, or make excuses and go elsewhere to avoid meeting them, not indicating an inability to repay. We believe that shops are reluctant to initiate litigation lightly until repeated demands have failed and have become unbearable. If they are sued in court, it is argued that the statute of limitations of two years has expired, regardless of whether the article applies to accounts owed directly to users by retail stores. It is far-fetched and treated as the right thing, then how are the legal interests of the store protected? This is why we have to request a clear explanation so that we can follow the law. The Chamber of Commerce believes that, according to the above circumstances, merchants have not given up their right to claim, and there are facts to prove that the statute of limitations is interrupted, which seems to be the natural interpretation. According to the circumstances described in the letter, we hereby prepare a document to be submitted to the esteemed court for interpretation, which would be convenient for the public.

Family of Lin Huiyuan

Yesterday's Reception for the Press in Shanghai 148

Cai Yuanpei and others, for the case of requesting the redress of injustice for the 19th Route Army regiment commander Li Jinduo's shooting of Longxi People's Education Center Director and Longxi Anti-Japanese Association Standing Committee Member Lin Huiyuan, now his family members Meng Yuan, etc., on the grounds that Huiyuan was wrongfully executed by Li Jinduo, with completely unfounded charges, abruptly silenced in the general public, specially came to Shanghai to appeal, so that the injustice would be made clear. Yesterday afternoon at 4 o'clock, at the Hua'an Building, they hosted members of the local press and the Civil Rights Protection Association, with more than 20 people attending. During the event, reports and speeches were given by the deceased Lin Huiyuan's descendants and Lin Mengwen, his father Lin Mengyuan, Lin Yutang, and others. Most of them said that the 19th Route Army, famous for its anti-Japanese stance, was transferred to Fujian to suppress bandits. At first, the people of Fujian all welcomed them, hoping they would come and take charge and relieve the people of Fujian from suffering. Unexpectedly, recently, their lower-level military officers have repeatedly engaged in the wrongful killing of innocent people, and Lin Huiyuan is just one of them, and so on. As for the cause of Lin's death, it was entirely because Lin severely punished the Taiwanese merchant Jian Mengchang, a doctor who purchased enemy goods, on May 5th, parading him in the streets and confiscating the property of his Gongji Hospital, leading to false accusations of collusion with bandits, resulting in his execution. The president of the local Civil Rights Protection Association, Song Qingling, had previously telegraphed Jiang Guangding, Cai Tingkai, and Chen Mingshu to intercede on his behalf. At the same time, about 20 people from the Shanghai literary and art circles, such as Cai Yuanpei, Liu Yazi, Lu Xun, and Yu Dafu, also issued a declaration, expressing the deep injustice of Lin's plight this time. The meeting adjourned after 5 o'clock. The telegrams and letters from Cai Yuanpei and others are recorded below:

Cai Yuanpei, Liu Yazi, Yang Xingfo, Lu Xun, Yu Dafu, Fu Sinian, Xia Gaizun, Ye Shengtao, Zhu Shaoping, Pan Guangdan, Sun Fuxi, Quan Zenggu, Li Qingya, Shao Xunmei, Yang Sao, Bai Wei, Zhang Yiping, Wu Shutian, Li Xiaofeng, Zhao Jingshen, and others' declaration for redressing the injustice of the Lin Huiyuan tragedy states: Recently, we saw in the newspapers that Lin Huiyuan, a standing committee member of the Longxi Anti-Japanese Association, was arrested on the 19th of last month on suspicion of colluding with bandits and executed by firing squad two hours later without any trial. We believe that Zhangzhou is not currently under martial law, so why was such a hasty disposition made? The news has caused a stir in southern Fujian, and it is rumored to be a suspicious case. When Huiyuan was in Shanghai, we all knew that he was straightforward in nature, and it was expected that he might offend local tyrants and be framed. Now, according to the report from his father Lin Mengwen, the concise case declaration from the Zhangzhou Anti-Japanese Association, and what was published in the Zhangzhou newspapers, we learned that there was a Taiwanese merchant named Jian Mengchang who, under the guise of local authority, purchased a large amount of enemy goods. Huiyuan, as a standing committee member of the Anti-Japanese Association, advocated strict punishment and expulsion from the country, even arguing to the point of resignation, and eventually paraded Jian in the streets. This was on May 5th. As for Huiyuan's execution, it was on May 19th. Jian Mengchang, a Taiwanese national, was not only not expelled from the country, but was instead protected, a complete reversal of justice. Moreover, Huiyuan's death was neither handed over to any court nor subjected to any trial, but was summarily executed by firing squad in the camp upon the written request of the special service regiment commander Li Jinbo. When escorted to the execution ground, his mouth was clamped with a wooden stick to prevent him from crying out his injustice. As for the accusation of collusion with the communists, there was no evidence other than the so-called confession of Gao Cun, and Gao Cun was also executed by firing squad on the same day with his mouth clamped with a wooden stick to silence him. The slightest clue is not difficult to find. At a time when the country is facing many difficulties, the result for those who sincerely resist Japan is like this. It is not only the misfortune of the deceased's family, but also the misfortune of our country. Therefore, we specially seek redress so that the outside world can understand the truth.

Song Qingling's telegram to Jiang, Cai, and Chen, seeking redress for Lin Huiyuan, states: To Chairman Jiang of the Fujian Provincial Government, and forwarded to Commander-in-Chief Cai and Mr. Chen Zhenru, Longxi Anti-Japanese Association Standing Committee Member Lin Huiyuan severely punished the Taiwanese traitor Jian Mengchang, who purchased a large amount of enemy goods, on May 5th, parading him in the streets. He was then executed by firing squad on the 19th by Regiment Commander Li on suspicion of colluding with bandits. He was neither handed over to any court for trial, nor was Gao Cun, who allegedly implicated him, executed at the same time with his mouth clamped with a wooden stick to silence him. The injustice is deep and cannot be cleared. We hope that you, gentlemen, upholding your consistent anti-Japanese aspiration, will thoroughly investigate and redress the injustice, so as to preserve your reputation and reassure the people. Song Qingling.

Cai Yuanpei's telegram to Jiang, Cai, and Chen, seeking redress for Lin Huiyuan, states: To Chairman Jiang of the Fujian Provincial Government, and forwarded to Commander-in-Chief Cai and Mr. Chen Zhenru, I previously read in the newspapers that Lin Huiyuan of Longxi was executed by firing squad for colluding with bandits. His father is also a loyal party member, and I have known his younger brother for many years. I cannot believe this and am greatly surprised. Recently, after consulting the newspapers and news from his family, I learned that the Taiwanese Jian Mengchang, under the guise of local authority, purchased a large amount of Japanese medicine. The Anti-Japanese Association decided to confiscate it and expel Jian from the country. Huiyuan, as a standing committee member, was framed by villains. Without any trial, he was unjustly killed with his mouth clamped, causing a sensation far and wide. It cannot but tarnish the glorious anti-Japanese reputation of your army. Could you thoroughly investigate and seek redress, so as to show fairness and encourage those who come after? This would be a great fortune for the Party and the country. Cai Yuanpei.

Association for the Cooperation of National Goods Production and Sales

Supporting the Implementation of New Tax Rates 149

The China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association sent a quick mail telegram to various departments of the government yesterday to support the implementation of the new customs tariff, stating: To the Nanjing Legislative Yuan, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry: Customs autonomy is a common practice in all countries around the world. The level of customs tariffs is the linchpin of the rise and fall of industries. The government authorities, in order to maintain the country's sovereignty and seek the welfare of the people, should increase import taxes to limit the influx of foreign goods, and reduce export taxes to encourage the export of domestic products. Policies should come from our own decisions, and powers should be controlled by ourselves. In an independent and sovereign country, how can foreign interference be allowed? Since the opening of our country to foreign trade, customs tariffs have been low, and sovereignty has not belonged to us. As a result, foreign goods have been imported at very low tax rates, with low costs and prices, flooding the markets. The Chinese people, limited by short-term gains, often enjoy using them. On the other hand, export tax rates have not been reduced, and the output of domestic products is burdened heavily. Not only are natural products affected, but also manufactured goods, because most of the raw materials are imported from foreign countries, bear a double burden of taxation, directly and indirectly, increasing costs and making exports difficult. It is even more difficult to compete with foreign goods. This is why it is difficult for our country's industries to flourish, and why strong neighbors are able to carry out their economic aggression. Since the National Government regained customs autonomy, it has been able to exert its own strength in eliminating obstacles and supporting industries. Although the new customs tariff has slightly increased import tax rates, it is still not up to par compared to other countries in the world. However, according to reports, various Japanese trade associations in this city have convened a general meeting and submitted a petition to Minister Arima, requesting him to forward it to our authorities, obstructing and hindering us. Upon hearing this, we are shocked and astonished. Customs autonomy is a common practice in all countries, and the promulgation of tariffs is a matter within the scope of internal affairs. How can foreign countries be allowed to interfere? Our people have been subjected to restrictions for decades, and once we want to liberate ourselves, the Japanese recklessly disregard justice, rely on force to threaten us, and attempt to continue to control our destiny. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? Our people, in order to fight for our own survival and for the country's sovereignty, can only unite and implore the government to firmly reject and severely condemn them in accordance with reason, so as to maintain sovereignty and cultivate the foundation of the country. We are willing to make any sacrifice and vow to be the backing of the authorities, so as to ensure thorough implementation without any retreat. We earnestly state our case and hope for your consideration. Respectfully, China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperation Association.

The Jiangsu Maritime Patrol Team directly under the Yangtze River Provincial Water Police Headquarters, on the pretext of issuing flag licenses and inspecting bandits in the waters where it is stationed, extorted flag license fees from fishing boats ranging from 30 to 50 yuan. Jiang Zhongzheng. (New Voice News Agency)

Dispute in the Hat-Making Industry Resolved 153

Yesterday morning, the Social Affairs Bureau mediated a dispute involving over sixty hat manufacturers in this city, including Dong Huasheng, Xu Yiyuan, and Xu Weiji. Due to the impact of the current situation, they changed the originally agreed-upon wages by offering discounts, which aroused opposition from the workers in various factories. The labor union requested mediation from the Social Affairs Bureau, but the matter remained unresolved. The Social Affairs Bureau sent personnel to investigate wages in various factories throughout the city to establish a standard for mediation. At 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the Social Affairs Bureau convened both labor and management for mediation. Wang Yuxiang and Li Xinfu represented the labor side's hat-making union, while Xu Senlin and Dong Guohua represented the management side's trade association. Tan Peiyan, a section member of the Social Affairs Bureau's Third Section, presided over the meeting. As a result, five measures were agreed upon: (1) For new-style straw edges, wages per dozen less than 60 cents will be calculated with a 20% increase, and those above 60 cents will be calculated with a 15% increase. (2) Wages that have already been settled, and those who are paid on a monthly basis or by piecework, are not subject to this rule. (3) If the labor is monthly and the term has been agreed upon by both parties, but the work has not yet expired, it will be calculated according to the following method: (A) If work is stopped after two months, one month's wages will be added (calculated as three months). (B) If work is stopped after three months, one month's wages will be added (calculated as four months). (C) If work is stopped after three and a half months, half a month's wages will not be added (calculated as four months). (D) If work is done for four months, no wages will be added (If five months have been specified, it will be calculated as five months. Temporary short-term labor is not subject to this rule.) (4) Apprentices will be calculated at 50% of the wages in the first year and 70% in the second year. (5) The various prices stipulated in the original contract for raw straw, coarse straw, and the original contract shall be calculated at 80% of the original contract. Both parties approved the measures at the time, and the dispute was resolved.

Taizhou Steamer Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 154

The Taizhou steamer, owned by the Lian'an Shipping Company's Taizhou Shipping Bureau, which was scheduled to sail the Haimen line today, was robbed by pirates on the Yangmian of Nanbeize outside Haimen port on the 24th of last month. The Taizhou steamer sailed from Haimen to Shanghai on the 31st of last month, passing through Shipu and Dinghai, and arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning, berthing at the Guanqiao Pier. The shipowner reported the details of the robbery and the fierce battle between the Huangyan and Wenling water police and the pirates. It is scheduled to operate as usual on the Shanghai-Haimen line today.

The Chinese Buddhist Association held its fifth National Buddhist Delegates Congress at the Gongdelin on Quansuxu Street at 10:00 AM yesterday. Swearing-in Ceremony 158

The sixteen executive committee members, including Yuan Ying and Wang Yiting, and the sixteen supervisory committee members, including the Norlha Living Buddha and the Zhangjia Living Buddha, were elected at 4:00 PM on the first day. Due to the lack of time, the swearing-in ceremony was postponed to yesterday. After being elected, Yuan Ying immediately resigned from the executive committee. After unanimous retention by the new and old committee members, he withdrew his resignation. Guanghua Petroleum Company

Will Sue the Municipal Council 160

=Regarding the Installation of Gasoline Pumps=

=Disagreement with the Municipal Council's View=

The "Da Mei Wan Bao" reported that, according to a letter from William, the lawyer representing Guanghua Petroleum Company, to the Municipal Council, the company is planning to sue the Consular Court, hoping to force the Municipal Council to allow the company to install gasoline pumps within the prohibited area of the International Settlement. The so-called prohibited area was established several years ago, stipulating that within the International Settlement, from the Bund westward to a straight line drawn along the racecourse's Avenue Edward Ezra, the installation of gasoline pumps and oil tanks under the sidewalks is prohibited, but the installation on private property is not subject to the ban. Mr. Chung Sze of the Municipal Council sent a letter to William, the representative lawyer of Guanghua, on April 25, stating that the Municipal Council has extensive powers over the city-owned property within the Settlement and has the power to manage roads within the Settlement and formulate traffic regulations in accordance with the bylaws. William then replied that he could not agree with the Municipal Council's view, believing that imposing a restriction on the installation of gasoline pumps within a certain distance, especially outside this distance, would effectively create a monopoly for certain oil companies and deny the same rights to other taxpayers. If the Municipal Council is unwilling to negotiate in order to ease the existing restrictions, it will appeal to the Consular Court and ask the Municipal Council to indicate its views on this matter.

Qiu Weiqing's Adopted Son

Qiu Changsheng Accused Again 161

│Prosecuted by Clan Chief Qiu Hengzhi│

=Accused of Embezzling Public Property and Falsifying Clan Genealogy=

=Authentic and Fake Genealogies and Obituary Serve as Evidence=

After the death of the giant dye merchant Qiu Weiqing, he left behind millions in property, currently managed by his adopted son Qiu Changsheng and his biological son Qiu Changyin. As a result, lawsuits have repeatedly arisen. Recently, Qiu Hengzhi, the Qiu clan chief, over sixty years old, stated that Qiu Weiqing had said before his death that he would use 100,000 yuan for clan charities, and 200,000 yuan would be given to the clan to be incorporated into the ancestral hall, to purchase charitable fields, charitable estates, and charitable schools, and that over 120 mu of Bazhou rake tree fields would be allocated to the ancestral hall. However, since Weiqing's death, all these funds have been embezzled by Qiu Changsheng alone and taken as his own. Furthermore, because he is an adopted son, fearing disapproval from the entire clan, since the clan genealogy once contained the adoption wording, he spent money to buy up the clan genealogy and fabricate a new genealogy. Qiu Changsheng's actions are illegal. Therefore, he hired lawyers Zheng Wenkai and others to submit a petition to the First Special Court, accusing Qiu Changsheng of embezzling public property and falsifying the clan genealogy, requesting that he be punished according to Articles 356 and 224 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qian Wenji opened the Second Criminal Court for questioning. First, the plaintiff Qiu Hengzhi explained the background, then lawyer Zheng further explained, and presented the authentic and fake genealogies, and Qiu Weiqing's obituary (containing wording about purchasing charitable fields, etc.) as evidence. When the defendant was questioned, he denied everything, saying that his father did not give any instructions regarding family matters when he passed away, so how could there be any mention of 300,000 yuan for charitable causes? He also hired lawyer Tao Jiachun for defense. The court stated that the case still required investigation and evidence, and ordered a postponement for further questioning.

Chaotic Wireless Broadcasts in This City 162

Negotiations with the Public Works Department to Impose Controls, According to the North China Daily News: Several representatives of wireless broadcasts in this city met with Mr. Fessenden, Secretary-General of the Public Works Department, on Wednesday, to discuss the chaotic wireless broadcasts in this city and the urgent need for controls. Mr. Fessenden requested that the representatives submit a written statement detailing the actual situation of wireless broadcasts, paying particular attention to avoiding technical difficulties in obstructing existing wavelengths, along with feasible solutions. He also expressed his willingness to present the matter to the Public Works Department's board meeting. However, it would be best to reach a friendly agreement to avoid mutual interference during broadcasts. He also stated that for the benefit of the public, the local authorities should discuss the matter to reach a mutual agreement and decision. In conclusion, to achieve a satisfactory solution, any measures should be implemented jointly with the Shanghai French Concession and the authorities.

This Year's Tea Inspection

New Standards Scheduled for Implementation 165

Implementation Starts on June 20th

Colored Tea Will Be Banned Simultaneously

The standards for the 22nd year of tea inspection and the measures for banning colored tea, after being resolved by the Commodity Inspection Technical Conference, have been submitted to the Ministry of Industry and approved for promulgation. The minimum inspection standards are similar to those of last year, but green tea has been changed to the No. 2 tea "Ben Hao Pearl Tea." The purpose of banning colored tea is to prohibit overly concentrated coloring and tea leaves containing toxic colorants. Because green tea for export, except for those shipped to America, is invariably colored, it not only hinders quality but is also harmful to health. The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, in order to maintain the long-standing reputation of Chinese tea and promote international trade, has specially complied with the order to implement new standards and measures for banning colored tea starting on June 20th of this year. It has already formulated three types of colored tea standards that should be banned, and one minimum standard for black tea, along with the new standards and measures.

Kidnapping Case in Wujiang Cracked in Shanghai 166

Four Kidnappers First Arrested in Shangxi Hotel

Hostage Rescued from Lane on Meixi Road Yesterday Morning

Shen Sibao's son, Changsheng, a resident of Beicaozhen, Wujiang County, just fifteen years old, was suddenly kidnapped by kidnappers on the 10th of last month. They then sent a letter to his family, demanding 2,000 yuan for ransom. Shen initially requested a reduction, but the kidnappers refused, so the ransom was gradually increased to 1,900 yuan, which the kidnappers then accepted. The handover location was arranged in this city. On the evening before last, detectives Pang Yutang and Li Shugui of the Zhabei Police Station learned that the kidnappers were hiding in Room 3 of the Shangxi Hotel on Fuzhou Road. They rushed to investigate and arrest them at 10:00 PM that night, and arrested four men and women on the spot: Zhang Laozhang (also known as Zhang Bao) from Suzhou, Jin A'er, Fei Jinbao, and a woman from Changzhou, Lu Zhaizhen. Under questioning back at the police station, the kidnappers confessed that the hostage Shen Changsheng was currently being held at No. 3, Lane 74, Meixi Road in the city. At 6:00 AM yesterday morning, Chinese and foreign detectives went to the location with the police district in charge, rescued the hostage, and arrested additional suspects, including Zhu Shuliang, Lin Hongchang, Zhou Shulin (i.e., Zhu Shulin), Shu Xiaodi, Shu Zhangshi, and several other men and women. They were temporarily detained at the police station. Zhang Laozhang and others were first escorted to the First Special District Local Court. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi appeared in court, recounted the process of solving the case, and requested that Zhang and others be temporarily detained, and requested that the Municipal Public Security Bureau be asked to transfer the remaining suspects so that the case could be investigated and prosecuted together. Judge Qian approved the request, briefly questioned Zhang and others, and ordered them to remain in custody pending the arrest of the remaining criminals for a scheduled hearing.

The circular letter regarding colored tea petition, etc., has been sent to all Chinese and foreign tea merchants in this city for attention. Hereafter, all kinds of tea leaves must pay attention to dryness and the source and name of the colorant used, so as not to cause mistakes. The 22nd-year tea inspection standards and colored tea banning measures are recorded below: (A) Minimum Inspection Standards 1. Green tea is based on Ping Shui No. 2 Tea and No. 7 Pearl Tea as the standard, and black tea is based on Hunan Second Red as the standard. The other various types of tea leaves are based on color, aroma, and palatability as the standard. 2. The moisture content of red and green tea is 8.5% as the standard, but this year green tea is qualified at 9% and black tea is qualified at 11%. The other various types of tea leaves are qualified at 12%. 3. The ash content of green and black tea is a maximum of 7% as the standard, but this year it is a maximum of 7.5% as qualified. (B) Colored Tea Banning Measures 1. When a merchant reports colored tea for inspection, the name of the colorant used must be clearly stated. When necessary, the analytical composition sheet of the colorant merchant may be ordered to be presented for inspection. 2. Tea leaves that are colored too strongly, similar to the formulated standard tea, or heavier, are prohibited from export. 3. Tea leaves that are colored with yellow lead chromate (commonly known as light yellow, three-fish yellow, Yiji yellow, etc.), green copper arsenite copper oxychloride (commonly known as sand green, etc.), and other toxic colorants are prohibited from export.

Improved National Product: French Gauze 171

Cotton cloth is a good material for making clothes. This kind of fabric was made by hand in the past, so the quality is inevitably rough and the color is also dull and dull. However, in the past, there was no new competition from imported goods, and the aesthetic psychology of the general public was not as developed as it is now. Therefore, seeing that cotton cloth is lighter and smoother than native cloth, everyone is happy to use it. Nowadays, machine-woven clothing is novel, beautiful, and dazzling, and it is full of the market. This kind of hand-made cotton cloth is difficult to stand on its feet. The Zhenxing Textile Factory, in view of this, deeply regrets the decline of domestic products, and thinks of ways to save it. The factory's textile technicians and chemical engineers carefully studied and adopted the latest German machines, and through careful chemical engineering, produced a new type of cotton cloth, which is light, soft, and smooth in texture, and the color is simple, elegant, and pleasant. It is called "French Gauze." The price is very cheap, which is very suitable for the economy of today's society. Therefore, since its production, simple and aesthetic female comrades have been vying to buy and use it, and they have praised it. It is a new contribution to the national products industry. The factory has a store in the Penglai Market, Xiaoximen. It is very convenient for local women who love national products to visit.

He Fangpu Has Now Been Released on Bail 172

All Accusations are Untrue The sugar merchant He Fangpu was previously arrested by the Zhejiang authorities on suspicion of something and sent to the Hangzhou Provincial Public Security Bureau. After that, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Lake Society, and the Haichang Guild, and other groups, sent telegrams to the Zhejiang Provincial Government to prove that Mr. He was honest and had no certain situation, requesting his release. Subsequently, the Zhejiang authorities conducted several interrogations and investigated the actual situation, knowing that although He had sold sugar goods at Mitsui & Co. before, he had completely cut off relations after September 18th. All the accusations were untrue. Therefore, he was granted bail.

Police Officer Committed Suicide Out of Grief for National Affairs 174

Tang Yongming Asked for Leave and Disappeared

The Life-Saving Bureau Retrieved the Body for Claim

Tang Yongming, a native of Beiping, 25 years old, was previously a police officer in the Beiping Municipal Public Security Bureau. Since the Shanghai War, Tang followed the team to Shanghai. Then, in May of last year, he was ordered to be transferred to the First District, First Precinct of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau as a third-class police officer. The police officer was very diligent in handling affairs on weekdays, and he was taciturn and rarely smiled, so he was highly valued by his superiors. However, recently, the military situation in Beiping was urgent, and Tang's family members lived in Beiping, so Tang was very worried, and often frowned and sighed repeatedly, and said to his colleagues that the national crisis was imminent, and the Japanese army was so barbaric, how would we live in the future? His colleagues did not pay attention. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 PM on the 29th of last month, Tang suddenly asked his superior for leave to go out for a bath, and never returned. The precinct reported the situation to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for approval. Unexpectedly, at about 8:00 PM the night before last, the patrol boat of the Tongren Fuyuantang Life-Saving Bureau at Nanmatou suddenly retrieved a male corpse from the nearby water, about twenty years old, wearing a white cloth short shirt, black pants, black thread socks on his feet, and colored shoes. He was brought back to the bureau for identification. It was then learned by the precinct, so they sent the police to inspect it. The deceased was the police officer Tang Yongming who had been missing for two days, who had committed suicide by throwing himself into the river. He immediately reported to the chief of the precinct, assigned a local headman, and reported to the Shanghai Local Court to ask for an autopsy, prepared a coffin for burial, and telegraphed his family to come to Shanghai to claim the body.

Inside the Dance Hall

Beauty Clashes with Russian 175

│A Handgun Without a License is Suspicious│

At 4:50 AM yesterday morning, inside the Dahua Dance Hall on Dongqiujiang Road, Zhabei, when the dancers were dancing happily, a beauty named Gao Bāluóbāsī suddenly had a conflict with a Russian named Aìbǐ Luósè because they disagreed. Gao punched Ai in the face, causing Ai's left eye to swell up immediately. At the same time, Ai took out a handgun from his pocket and tried to fire at Gao. Gao, upon seeing this, had nowhere to escape, so he shouted for help. The police officer on duty at Post No. 5 of the First Precinct of the Fifth District heard this, and rushed in to see the situation. He bravely stepped forward and snatched the handgun from Ai. He saw that it contained seven bullets. He searched his body again and found four more bullets. He asked if he had a gun license, but he hesitated. He was taken to the First Precinct and reported. Liang Fuchu, the director of the precinct, personally interrogated him, but the Russian never handed over a gun license. At the same time, there were four more bullets hidden in his pocket, which was suspicious. He was first sent to the nearby Fumin Hospital to examine his injuries, and then, at about 1:00 PM, he, along with the guns and bullets, was transferred to the Third Section of the General Bureau for questioning. The beauty Gao Bāluóbāsī was also sent to the Diswei Road Police Station for processing at the same time.

Chai Yanxu's False Accusation 176

│Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment with Probation│

Chai Bingsheng, a wealthy merchant from Huzhou, had accumulated a great deal of wealth during his lifetime, especially jewelry. When he and his wife died one after another, his son Yanxu was still young, so he entrusted his close relatives Pan Xiangsheng and Ji Zhongren to take care of him. All the deeds and jewelry were stored in the Xingye Bank for safekeeping by Pan and others. Pan was Yanxu's uncle and Ji was his cousin, so they could not refuse. Ten years ago, Pan and Ji thought that Chai Yanxu had grown up and that they could unload their responsibility for safekeeping, so they returned all the items clearly. Unexpectedly, recently, Chai Yanxu hired lawyers Qin Liankui and Chang Zhihao to file a criminal lawsuit against Pan and Ji, saying that they had embezzled property. Pan and others said that the ornaments they were in charge of had already been returned, but Chai actually repaid kindness with hatred, which was intolerable. They also hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to not only clarify the facts, but also filed a counterclaim against Chai Yanxu, asking for him to be punished for false accusations. After several times of summoning both parties and witnesses by the First Special District Local Court for investigation, the judge persuaded them to reconcile because the two sides were close relatives. However, Pan and others believed that Chai's actions were not only fabricated and falsely accused, but also intentionally damaged their reputation, and finally it was impossible to settle peacefully. Now the case has been tried and concluded. Yesterday afternoon, the presiding judge opened the court and announced the verdict. Pan and Ji were both innocent. Chai Yanxu's false accusation was true. He was sentenced to two months in prison to warn him, but he was given probation for two years because it was his first time.

The book's value can be seen from these inscriptions. It has now been published and is sold on consignment by Zuozhe Bookstore on Sima Road, Limin Bookstore, and Qingyun Bookstore Company. It is divided into two types: Chinese binding and Western binding, each in two thick volumes, priced at two yuan and one yuan respectively.

No Way Out 193

││Letter from Zhao Yujun of Wujin││

Every day I see you gentlemen solving difficult problems for readers, and now it's my turn ││ Actually, it's a problem faced by most of the business community, currently oppressed by the Business Tax Bureau to the point of having no way out. I know that discussing this now will not help the overall situation. But this is the groan of the masses, and it is worth discussing!

This year, twenty-one of the twenty-seven money houses in Changzhou City have already collapsed, and the remaining six are in constant turmoil. Other industries are also closing down more than opening, and the decline of the business community can be imagined! The sharp increase in unemployed youth and the hardship of ordinary people's lives are not even considered by the so-called public servant officials? Recently, the squeezing has become even more severe. For example, the recent business tax: goods of category A are taxed at 5 per thousand, and if sold to category B, category B must also be taxed at 5 per thousand; if category B resells to category C, category C must be taxed at 5 per thousand again; sold repeatedly, taxed layer by layer; regardless of whether they are luxury goods or daily necessities for ordinary people, and those who have already paid national tax are also subject to tax, alas! Is the original intention of national taxation like this?

[Oppressive government is fiercer than a tiger, and corrupt officials are more poisonous than snakes;] I think now it is the Republic of China, and the government is definitely not a tiger? Officials are not poisonous snakes? They are our public servants. If public servants do something wrong, the masters should come out to correct them. Is that good or not? Respectfully ask the │talented│ editor: (1) Is opposing harsh taxes endangering the Republic of China? (2) Are goods that have already paid national tax obligated to pay business tax? (3) If [poisonous snakes] bite people, what method should we use to eliminate them?

Answer: The social phenomenon described in the letter is a realistic picture of the widespread bankruptcy in China today. Not only is Changzhou like this, but Zhenjiang is also like this. There are several dozen money houses in Zhenjiang, but only six or seven are listed this year. As for the banks, they are still the same, and even added one or two. From this, we can at least see: ㈠ The trend of China's usurious capital and commercial capital being swallowed up by banking capital: ㈡ Rural bankruptcy, farmers unable to repay debts, the silk and yarn industries in the Suhangchang area went bankrupt, and most of the cash flowed out from the inland, returning to Shanghai. The inland money houses are unable to circulate, and nineteen out of ten are closing down. Not only are Zhen and Chang like this, but other major cities such as Hangzhou, Hankou, Nanjing, and Shanghai are also like this. "The government is definitely not a tiger? Officials are definitely not poisonous snakes?" The decision of this kind of question should not be based on its name ││ the so-called "public servant" ││ but should be based on its facts; it should not be based on its announcements, but should be based on its administration. The remaining three questions are answered together as follows: ㈠ Opposing harsh taxes is definitely not "endangering the Republic of China"; not only does it not endanger it, but it also maintains it. Because a true republic absolutely does not allow harsh taxes, and tolerating harsh taxes, even rewarding harsh taxes with "officials competing for profit from top to bottom," is definitely not a republic but an enemy of the republic. ㈡ In theory, goods that have already paid national tax should not be subject to any taxes. Even if there is a need to levy tax out of necessity, the people must understand, trust, and promise that this tax is for the country and for the people. If the people only have the obligation to pay taxes but have no way to understand, let alone trust, and even have no right and opportunity to promise or reject this tax, then the people, according to the law, have no obligation to pay harsh taxes at all. ㈢ If it is really a poisonous snake, it will definitely bite people, and we should eliminate it. The ancient Chinese had a saying, "To kill a snake, strike at its seven inches" │ this saying still has considerable significance today. However, we must know that the poisonous snakes today are not one, but a group. Then, the method of killing snakes today can no longer be thought of as an individual action, that is to say, it can no longer be eliminated by individual strength. Only by uniting can we eliminate this group of snakes.

Calculation of Grid Bias Resistor 194

Xiang

Whether a vacuum tube is used for high-frequency or low-frequency amplification, there must be a proper negative voltage on the grid. There are two sources of this negative voltage: the first is to use a set of C batteries connected in the grid circuit to supply it; the second is to use a resistor connected in the grid circuit, using the voltage drop generated when the plate current passes through this resistor to supply it. AC radios on the market all use the second method. The resistance value of this resistor is very important and must be accurate, otherwise the effectiveness of the vacuum tube will be completely lost. The calculation method is as follows:

Grid Resistor 195

㈠ Calculation Method of Resistance Value

First, check the required grid voltage and plate current values of the vacuum tube on the specification sheet of various vacuum tubes (this sheet is included in the instruction manual when purchasing the vacuum tube and in radio books). According to Ohm's law, divide the grid voltage by the plate current. The quotient obtained is the resistance value that this grid bias resistor should have. If it is a screen-grid vacuum tube, the screen-grid current must also be included in the plate current calculation. For example, for a 247 vacuum tube, the grid negative voltage should be 16.5 volts, the plate current is 31 milliamperes, and the screen-grid current is 6 milliamperes, then the grid bias resistor should be 16.5/(0.031 + 0.006) = 445 ohms.

㈡ Calculation Method of Resistor Power Size

When purchasing a resistor, in addition to the resistance value, you should also pay attention to the power it can withstand. The unit of power is watts. The calculation method is also very simple. Just multiply the current by itself and then multiply by the resistance value. The product is the size of the power. For example, the power of the resistor in the previous example should be 0.0372 x 445 = 0.6 watts. In actual application, for safety, it is best to use a resistor three times the power, so the power limit marked on this resistor should be two watts.

Self-Made High Resistance 196

Qi

The components used in radio equipment seem very complicated at first glance, but when summarized, in addition to vacuum tubes, most of them are capacitors, coils, and resistors, connected in circuits, with endless changes.

There are many publications in books and magazines about the making of capacitors and coils. However, there is still little self-made information about resistors. The reasons are (1) it is not easy to measure its resistance, (2) it is not heat-resistant (that is, the power in watts is not large), but according to my experiments, the high resistance used in ordinary radios (mostly AC ones) is less than one watt. For example, in a three-tube radio, the step-down resistor used in the detector tube is about 40,000 ohms, and the current passing through it is at most 5 milliamperes (5MA). If it is a 27 vacuum tube, the current during detection is less than 3 milliamperes, then the inherent watts of the above resistor is 12 x R (0.003) 2 x 40,000 = 0.36W. According to the above formula, it can be known that the heat resistance of the resistor is directly proportional to its resistance B at equal current.

Now let's talk about the making method. Speaking of fixed ones, the materials needed are just a few good matches (according to the experiment, the domestic product "Meili" brand is the best), thick ink, a 6B or soft pencil, and a small square of thin copper sheet. For the making method, first soak the match in ink so that it is completely soaked and dried. If the resistance needs to be very large, such as 2Meg or 1/2Meg, then there is no need to apply lead again, but sometimes a little is also needed. If it is 40,000 ohms, then it must be fully coated. Then cut the thin copper skin into a convex shape and wrap it on the match (Figure 1). According to the above method, it can also be said to be semi-variable. Just move the copper sleeve to change its distance. The closer it is, the smaller the resistance, or vice versa. The experiment has shown that when the match is fully coated with black lead, at 40,000 ohms, it is about one centimeter (cm) apart, and at about 1,000 ohms (used as a substitute C battery), the closer the two are, the better. However, there is no fixed ratio between the resistance and its distance, because the amount of lead varies greatly and must be determined by experiment. If you want it to be more perfect, you can hide this resistor in a thin glass tube and seal both ends with sealing wax.

Sometimes we need to use variable ones, such as for volume control (around ro, ooo｜Ioo｀ooo ohms), for push-pull control, and potentiometers, etc., then you can follow the second diagram to do it. The materials are also very economical. The disc is made of hard rubber. About one-fourth thick is enough. Punch a hole in the middle: or remove the resistance wire from the old variable resistor. Various making methods will be very clear after looking at the second diagram. Its function is to move the copper skin on the absorbent paper, indirectly changing its distance. Whether to apply lead or not is the same as the fixed one and must be experimented with yourself. Due to space limitations, I cannot elaborate more. The method of measuring high resistance will be described in detail in another article.

Figure 1

S Match

B Convex Copper Skin

If tin foil is sandwiched between the copper skin and the match, it will be easier to conduct electricity and more heat-resistant.

Figure 2

L Thick Absorbent Paper

A Copper Strip

D Hard Rubber Disc

C Copper Movable Contact CDA

Simple Lightning Arrester 197

Zhang Guoquan

Now that the weather is getting hotter, lightning often occurs. Anyone with an antenna should have a lightning arrester to prevent it. Now I will introduce a lightning arrester that costs very little and has the same effect as those sold on the market. You might as well give it a try. The making method is as follows:

Prepare a piece of copper sheet three inches long and two inches wide, a piece of wood, and two screws. First, use scissors to cut the copper sheet into very sharp canine teeth. Cut two pieces of copper sheet in the same way and screw one end onto the wood with screws. The pointed teeth should be as close as possible, but not touching, to form a short circuit. Once made according to the above method, the lightning arrester is successful. Its wiring is shown in the left figure.

AC Radio Inspection Method 200

Cheng Quan

What makes people most unhappy when playing with AC radios is that the radio has various faults, such as AC hum, constant crackling, or even no sound at all. When you encounter this situation, you have to repair it yourself. But although it is not difficult to start, it is not very easy to find out where the defect is. Often, one symptom has more than a dozen causes. Moreover, the internal circuit of the radio is complex and the wiring is chaotic, which makes people more easily at a loss. The author will now introduce an inspection method. If you check according to the method, even the most subtle places can be easily detected. You only need to prepare a DC voltmeter. This meter must be able to measure zero to six volts and zero to two hundred volts. And two connecting wires. For the sake of simple explanation, take the final stage of an ordinary AC radio as an example and explain it separately.

The figure shows the final stage amplification and power supply section. T is the final stage low-frequency transformer, Vi is the amplifier tube, V2 is the rectifier tube, P.T. is the power transformer, AFC is the choke coil, C1C2 are the filter capacitors, R2 is the substitute C resistor, C3 is the bypass capacitor, and R1 is the center resistor (some do not use the center resistor because the power transformer already has a center tap). The inspector should first turn on the radio and then check its plate, grid, and filament circuits separately.

Plate Circuit 201

Connect the negative pole of the voltmeter to point 11 of R1, and connect the positive pole of the high-voltage end (that is, the zero to two hundred volt section of the voltmeter) to point 2 in the figure. At this time, the speaker is not connected, so the pointer on the meter does not move. If the speaker is connected and the meter pointer still does not move, you can change the positive wire to point 3. If the pointer moves, the speaker coil is broken. If the pointer still does not move, change to point 5. If the meter pointer moves, the AFC is broken. If the pointer still does not move, then change to point 6. If the pointer moves, there is a break in the connection between 6 and 5. If the pointer still does not move, the rectifier tube is broken. Try replacing it with a new one. If the pointer still does not move, the high-voltage wire of the power transformer is damaged or C1C2 is short-circuited. At this time, or change the negative pole of the voltmeter to the ground wire. If the meter pointer moves, R1 is damaged.

Grid Circuit 202

Change the voltmeter to the low-voltage section (that is, zero to six volts). Connect the negative pole to point G in the figure and connect the positive pole to point Ⅱ. You can measure a voltage of about two volts. Then the grid circuit is undamaged. If the meter pointer does not move, C3 must be short-circuited or R2 must be broken.

Filament Circuit 203

The filament circuit of an AC radio is alternating current, so a DC voltmeter cannot be used to measure the correct voltage value. However, you can usually determine it by looking at the brightness of the filament. If the vacuum tube is not bright, you can replace it with a new one (or use the light bulb in a flashlight as a substitute). If it is still not bright, then the power transformer or the wiring is broken.

The above is all about the final stage, but the primary and secondary stages are the same. You can check them according to the steps described above. As for the order of checking the three circuits, it depends on the symptoms. If the light is not on, check the filament circuit first. If it is bright but there is no sound, check the plate circuit first. If there is sound but it is not clear, or there is noise, check the grid circuit first. Finally, there are a few words to pay attention to.

㈠ When a radio has symptoms, you must first check the antenna, ground, and lightning arrester.

㈡ After checking out one defect, you must check whether there are other defects.

㈢ Each time, record it for future reference.

AC Radio

Method to Avoid Strange Noises 204

Li Yuanqing

When experimenting with AC radios yourself, it is often easy to generate many strange noises. The following are the most common types:

(1) Regenerative radios are most sensitive to receiving external broadcasts when they are about to oscillate. However, at this time, a kind of "pat-pat" sound similar to the sound of a gasoline boat releasing air (Motorboating) often occurs, disturbing the correct sound and is very annoying. The remedy is to first reduce the detector's B voltage. If it is ineffective, replace the bypass capacitor of the detector B voltage with a 2mf one (see Figure 1). (2) When the radio is about to oscillate, in addition to the above-mentioned sound, sometimes a long whistling sound (Frinkhow) (roughly in the shorter wavelength range) will also occur. If a 0.1｀2Meg ohm resistor is connected in parallel on the secondary coil of the first-stage low-frequency amplifier transformer, it can be avoided. This kind of noise can also be avoided in the same way when it occurs in DC radios (see Figure 2).

(3) Sometimes a noise occurs when the radio is first turned on, and it returns to its original state after the filament heats up. Although this special phenomenon is harmless, it is still annoying. The remedy is the same as in item 2.

(4) When the radio does not oscillate, a noise occurs, but not when it oscillates. The method to avoid it is to lay a piece of copper skin on the bottom of the box and connect the copper skin to the ground wire.

In addition, if the grid circuit is close to the plate circuit, the detector tube does not use a shield, and the grid leak value is too small... various noises can also occur. Due to space limitations, I will not elaborate on them here.

Soochow University Eighth Anniversary 219

Soochow University is celebrating its anniversary today and has a special holiday. Yesterday's issue specially carried:

Opinions on What Provincial and County Education Bureaus Should Preserve 220

Since the internal affairs conference proposed changing the county organization law, increasing the authority of county magistrates, and changing the various sections, various provinces have followed suit, and many have already implemented it.

Whether changing bureaus to sections is better than establishing separate bureaus is not discussed here. But taking the change of the education bureau to a section of the county government as an example, analyzing it from the aspects of theory, history, facts, national conditions, and numbers, it is really not appropriate.

In theory, education is a specialized undertaking, not comparable to other ordinary political affairs. Educational administration must be presided over by someone familiar with education in order to be enthusiastic and competent. The county magistrate is an ordinary official, not familiar with education. Once charged with educational administration, it is easy to be neglected due to different concepts, or even if it is not neglected, the situation is still unfamiliar, and the measures are inevitably inappropriate.

Historically, since the establishment of schools in China, except for a few provinces, the educational administration of various counties has been managed by separate bureaus. This has been the case for decades. Even in the old imperial examination era, each county had educational officials such as instructors and guides to manage educational affairs, which were always separate from ordinary administration. The situation in European and American countries is also the same. Local educational administration is often set up in bureaus or other similar bodies, clearly separated from ordinary administration. Even the Shanghai Special District now has a so-called [Chinese Education Department] to manage schools, without entrusting the so-called [Chinese education] to ordinary officials. In fact, in a few provinces in China, the educational administration of various counties does not have a separate education bureau, but the establishment of schools is far less than in provinces with bureaus, and the educational achievements are also far less than in provinces with bureaus. According to investigations, in a certain province, some counties have changed bureaus to sections, and some county magistrates or administrative commissioners have misappropriated education funds, and some have disregarded education laws and insisted on their own ideas. Even county magistrates who are somewhat knowledgeable about education are struggling to discuss school affairs with principals and are too busy to have any plans for education. The facts are all there and cannot be denied.

Regarding national conditions, education in China is still in its infancy. Having a separate bureau is still worried about being constrained by ordinary administration, unable to concentrate on developing education and making long-term progress. Therefore, after the League of Nations Education Inspection Group came to China to inspect education, they suggested [educational administration should be further free from interference from ordinary administration] and advocated that [the heads of county education bureaus should be appointed by the provincial education department]. This shows a deep understanding of China's national conditions, not only advocating the establishment of bureaus to manage educational administration, but also wanting it to be completely free from the interference of county magistrates.

Some say, [Changing bureaus to sections can save more money in terms of expenses. This is a last resort when local governments are empty.] However, setting up a bureau has a director, supervisors, staff, and secretaries, while changing to a section still has a section chief, supervisors, staff, and secretaries. There is no significant difference in the number of people and their treatment. Moreover, if the funds are small, the scope can be small. What is the difference between setting up a bureau and a section?

Some also say, [After changing bureaus to sections, the section chief can be directly appointed by the provincial education department, without being completely controlled by the county magistrate, which is still equivalent to setting up a bureau.] However, working in the same organization, the section chief is ultimately a subordinate. If their views differ from the county magistrate, opposing them would be considered insubordinate, while following them would be uneasy. Between going and staying, there are many obstacles. Moreover, if changing bureaus to sections does not create any obstacles and is still equivalent to setting up a bureau, then why bother with this unnecessary move? Based on the above reasons, it is advocated that the existing county education bureaus that have been changed to sections should be restored as soon as possible within a possible scope. Those that have not yet established bureaus should also consider establishing them at an appropriate time. The government should clearly stipulate that the principle of county educational administration should be to establish bureaus to manage it, and no matter how the county organization law changes, this principle should be preserved and not replaced, in order to emphasize education and assign responsibilities.

The 19th Route Army football team is strong and well-equipped. With the addition of Jiang Meijing and Zhong Yongsen, they are even more impressive. Seventy to eighty percent of the game was spent attacking and surrounding. The only regret is that they could not score the final goal as they wished. The wings contributed greatly, and the center was also excellent. The center back line and inner defense advanced and retreated in an orderly manner. In the future, with the addition of Feng Jingxiang, Tan Jiangbai, Li Tiansheng, and Zhu Guolun, their strength will be so tenacious that it will be beyond our expectations.

The Fudan Team Resists a Strong Enemy 232

The Fudan team, the champion of the China Football League, encountered a strong enemy for the first time yesterday, like a lone boat struggling in a storm. Fortunately, the entire army gave their all, and they were able to reach the other shore safely and end the match in a draw. At the beginning of the contact between the two armies, they attacked three times and were once very powerful. However, before long, the difference in strength gradually became clear, so they retreated to strategic passes and adopted a defensive strategy. All eleven people did their best, especially goalkeeper Yang Mingjin, who had extraordinary skills. However, once the city gate was wide open and the ball hit the wooden post, and once it was only a foot away from the goal, but the ball was shot high into the sky. Furthermore, there were three penalty kicks, but they turned bad luck into good fortune. This was not without good fortune.

The Back-and-Forth Lasted a Long Time Without a Winner 233

Referee Shen Huichun blew his silver whistle, and the clouds of war rose. The Fudan team waited at their ease and had many advantages. Five minutes later, the forwards attacked three times, but failed repeatedly due to lack of coordination. Zhou Shaowen, Yu Shunzhang, and Feng Nianhan were all formidable. Jiang Shanjing was bold and powerful. The 19th Route Army's defense had this pillar, so although there were many alarms, the fire did not spread. Before long, Fudan midfielder Wang Shusen was transporting military supplies during the kickoff when he was intercepted by Xu Yaoguang, who passed it to Yang Benhan. This led to an uprising in the eastern suburbs, which was difficult to quell, so he had no choice but to kick the ball far away. Huang Meishun failed to make a decisive decision and missed the opportunity.

Yu Shunzhang Misses Twice 234

The Fudan soldiers were all shocked. Black-faced General Zhang Ke roared angrily, and the ball broke through the encirclement. Huang Shunyue failed to attack, and Yu Shunzhang and Hong Nianhan supported each other and advanced in a linked manner, entering the encirclement in an instant. Jiang Shanjing and Zhou Dayun were entangled, and Yu Shunzhang was in the best position, but he could not shoot. How frustrating! Two minutes later, Hong Nianhan could have sent a ball to the 19th Route Army's goal, but Yu Shunzhang was one step slower, and the military was formed with old fists, and the ball was released dangerously.

The 19th Route Army Attacks Fervently But Fails 235

The sides switched again, and the 19th Route Army's forwards were radiant. In the Fudan penalty area, the artillery fire was earth-shattering, and the situation was full of dangers. Wang Shusen hurriedly transferred Zhao An and the other two generals back to help defend. Yu Shunzhang and Feng Nianhan also took the opportunity to rush to the rear defense to help block. There were many obstacles in the kickoff line. Zhong Yongsen and Zheng Shaokang went in and out ten times, but it was difficult to achieve success. Huang Meishun was under the strict surveillance of Wang Shusen and found it difficult to fight. In the end, they could not open the deadlock, and the match ended 0-0.

│Reception for the 19th Route Army Football Team│

The 19th Route Army Youth Service Corps held a reception last night at the Da Jiali Hotel for the Shanghai press and sports circles. Wang Xiaolai, Hu Fengxiang, Yang Pufu, and Zhou Fuzhang, the senior advisors of the corps, Jin Huating, the representative of the Journalists Association, Chen Bingde, the director of sports at Fudan, Yu Hengzhi, the director of sports at Jinan, reporters from Shen Bao, Shi Bao, Xinwen Bao, Shishi Xinbao, and Chen Bao, and players from Jinan and Fudan, a total of more than 80 people, gathered together in a lively atmosphere. After several rounds of drinks, Jin Yiting, the head of the corps, gave a welcome speech. Then, Secretary Wu Qinyao stood up to report on the organization of the corps and the mission of the football team in Shanghai. He said that this time, the 19th Route Army vanguard team volunteered to resist Japan. The head of our corps, Jin Yiting, and the youth of Guangdong Province sacrificed their original positions in order to fulfill their national responsibilities and followed the troops to participate in the work in the war zone. Their biggest goal is to save the country and the nation. The corps is divided into five sections (propaganda, transportation, medical care, general affairs, and sports) to cooperate and work together. The first batch of corps members has already departed from Guangdong with the first column commander Zhang Yan and has reached Chenzhou, Hunan Province. The second batch of corps members includes many famous football players from Nanhua, led by Shan Jingyuan, the head of the sports section, to Shanghai to prepare for competitions along the way. On the one hand, they will use this to arouse the public to participate in the anti-Japanese work together, and on the other hand, they will raise funds through competitions to help war refugees and purchase medical supplies. Unfortunately, things did not go as planned. When the football team arrived in Shanghai, there were no opponents. Our corps always thought that the China National Sports Association was the highest sports organization in the country. When the football team arrived in Shanghai, they immediately visited Mr. Shen Siliang, the main person in charge, hoping that the association would help. Our corps came to Shanghai for the first time and did not understand the situation here. After several negotiations, the association was afraid that there would be political implications, which caused obstacles. Secondly, because the football season has ended, they could not gather the team to help. Fortunately, the two friendly teams of Jinan and Fudan could not bear to see our team make an empty trip and agreed to play a friendly match. The others who wanted to compete with our team were disappointed because there was no venue. The second batch of warriors of our team will arrive in Shanghai during the day. We don't know if Donghua, who is returning to the country, will have a good opportunity to meet with them. Our corps has a major mission and needs the guidance of all comrades in many places. We sincerely hope that you will use your patriotic enthusiasm to give us guidance so that we can prepare. This time, the football team came to Shanghai, and we are grateful to our corps advisor Mr. Wang Xiaolai and all the comrades in the press for their help. We would like to express our sincere gratitude.

Fudan Volleyball Team Defeats Soochow 238

The Fudan University volleyball team has been famous in Jiangnan for more than ten years. The team recently plans to go to Singapore. Yesterday afternoon, they specially invited the Soochow University team to Jiangwan for a friendly match. As a result, Fudan won 3-2. The scores were 18-21, 21-12, 21-18, 18-21, 21-14. The referee was Tan Tianpei. Also, the B team did not play because the John High School team did not arrive.

Starting Problem

Should Not Accommodate Foreigners 246

There are two starters for this competition, one is the American Hall and the other is our Chinese Jiang Xiangqing. All participating countries requested that the starting commands be given according to the rules of the United States and Britain, that is, the gun is fired immediately after the ready command, without the commands of "On your marks," "Set," and a two-second delay before firing. Shen Siliang, the general secretary of the Athletic Association, has agreed to use the rules of the United States and Britain, otherwise, foreigners will suffer too much. However, if the rules of the United States and Britain are used, our Chinese athletes will inevitably be greatly restricted. Shen Siliang specifically instructed Jiang Xiangqing to contact Hall to discuss how the two should cooperate. However, Mr. Jiang has not yet met Hall and needs to discuss it further after arriving at the venue today. According to the international rules of track and field, the starting commands should be given in the language of the country where the games are held. At the previous Far Eastern Games held in Japan, all starting commands were given in Japanese. Therefore, according to international rules, the starting commands at the Shanghai All Nations Games should be given in our Chinese language. It is even more inappropriate to adopt the rules of the United States and Britain. Now that English is already being used, it is already a great accommodation. If we have to use the rules of the United States and Britain again, it would be too much of an accommodation to foreigners and a lack of self-respect. According to Jiang Xiangqing, there may be some disputes over the starting rules. If it is decided that the rules of the United States and Britain must be used, then Mr. Jiang will voluntarily give up and is unwilling to serve as the starter. It is hoped that our Chinese athletes will pay special attention.

Hopes of Various Countries 247

The situation and hopes of the nine countries can be described as follows based on pre-event observations: (1) China: China's greatest advantage is the average talent level. Even if there is little hope of winning first place in each event, its position will definitely be higher than other countries. This year, there are many good players from various countries, and their strength will be dispersed. China has a better chance. There will definitely be positions in the short and long-distance races. The good players in the hurdles from the United States and Britain have already left Shanghai, so we can win steadily. In the two throws, there are Guan Wanyu and Leng Peigen. In the jumping events, Chen Ling, Gu Huo, and Wu Jinqi will not be disappointed.

(2) Britain: Britain's championship last year relied entirely on track events. Now, these good players have been transferred elsewhere. They were selected from Argar and Lancashire. In the short-distance races, Sheppard and Gregg are recommended. In the long-distance races, Kennatai is indeed a good player.

(3) America: America is China's greatest rival, but it is not at its peak this year. The good players are not improving, and the veterans are getting old. The most promising are: (1) Servis, who is a student at Oberlin College in the United States. His 800-meter record is exactly two minutes. He is participating in the 800-meter and 1500-meter races. (2) Yelashe, who is very good at short-distance running. (3) Laores, also a short-distance runner. (4) Hertesheng, a good javelin thrower, holds the meet record of 47.65 meters.

(4) Russia: There are many good players, but not many in number, and only one or two in the hurdles and short-distance races. There is little hope for championships, but the positions should be in the top three or four. Noteworthy are: (1) Tomoshevsky, 100 meters in 11.5 seconds, (2) Motovkin, steady first in the shot put, 12.72 meters, (3) Minolov in the discus throw, (4) Lotrenkov in the middle distance, and (5) Tatariev in the 10,000 meters.

(5) Germany: Not many in number, but the football star of West, Pike, is the leader. Pike was selected as a German Olympic representative but did not attend. He is particularly good at the shot put. There is also Krammer's discus, which will definitely have a position.

(6) The Japanese are not many, but they are all ruthless generals. Mr. Oka is the leader. He attended the Far Eastern Games this time. His highest record in the 100 meters is 10.8 seconds, which is worthy of attention. The next is Komatsu's triple jump, Furukawa's high jump and javelin. It is said that there are also good players in the hurdles. Let's wait and see.

(7) The French, Jewish, and Latvian representatives are all from the stationed troops in Shanghai. Their results are unknown. Jewish and Latvia each have only one person and are not very important. (8) The women's championship is likely to be won by Britain and America, with America having a higher chance. Bernat's high jump of 1.39 meters is unmatched. Her four-meter loss to Zhuang Mingzhen. Britain's Thompson will definitely win two short-distance events. Her 13.2-second 100 meters is unmatched by China. It is hoped that the heroines of China will work hard to excel.

Scoring Method 248

The team scores include men's and women's championships. In each event, the top four are recorded. The scoring method uses a 5-3-2-1 system. The relay is doubled. The team with the most points wins the overall championship. Track and field events are not separated. Individual scores are not counted.

The executive committee of the congress previously decided that the first place will be awarded a silver cup, with a value not exceeding 20 yuan. The second, third, and fourth places will be awarded commemorative medals. It has now been decided that, to encourage participation, the second place will also be awarded a small silver cup.

Conference News 249

Releasing Pigeons: This time, the News Daily will release more than 60 pigeons with colored ribbons tied to their feet during the opening ceremony to create a grand spectacle and express the meaning of peace. This is often an innovation in our country and adds color to the conference.

Military Music Broadcast: The conference site's announcements will be broadcast by the [Standard] and [Wheeler] companies' broadcasting machines, and the US military Mack Lin's military band will come to the site to play, adding interest. The order of the conference site will be maintained by the Guanghua Boy Scouts.

Notice to Team Members: Members of the Chinese team must gather in the basketball room at 11:00 AM to distribute number cloths and uniforms. All conference staff and athletes are requested to arrive at the site at 1:15 PM to prepare to participate in the opening ceremony and parade (scheduled to be held at 1:30 PM). To ensure uniformity in the venue, all staff should preferably wear dark-colored tops and white trousers.

Visiting Routes: Tickets are divided into two types: one yuan and six jiao. One-yuan tickets enter the venue from the Zhaobang Road entrance, and six-jiao tickets enter the venue from the west side of the basketball room at the Maron Road entrance.
